Used to validate RFC compliance for various HTTP protocol elements.\n     8→\n     9→namespace Envoy {\n    10→namespace Http {\n    11→\n    12→inline constexpr bool testCharInTable(const std::array<uint32_t, 8>& table, char c) {\n    13→  // CPU cache friendly version of a lookup in a bit table of size 256.\n    14→  // The table is organized as 8 32 bit words.\n    15→  // This function looks up a bit from the `table` at the index `c`.\n    16→  // This function is used to test whether a character `c` is allowed\n    17→  // or not based on the value of a bit at index `c`.\n The validation occurs at multiple levels:\\n\\n**Header Validation Logic (source/common/http/header_utility.cc/.h):**\\n- `headerNameIsValid()`: Validates header names against RFC 7230 character sets, checking for valid token characters. Uses character tables from character_set_validation.h. For pseudo-headers (starting with ':'), delegates to nghttp2 or quiche validation.\\n- `headerValueIsValid()`: Validates header values using http2::adapter::HeaderValidator, allowing obsolete text per RFC.\\n- `checkValidRequestHeaders()`: Performs comprehensive validation of all header entries in a request, checking both names and values for forbidden characters (embedded NULLs, newlines, etc.).\\n- `requestHeadersValid()`: Validates specific headers (Host, Method, Scheme) for authority compliance and proper formatting.\\n- `isRemovableHeader()` / `isModifiableHeader()`: Prevents removal/modification of pseudo-headers (starting with ':') and the Host header, which are critical for HTTP semantics.\\n\\n**Internal Header Stripping (source/common/http/conn_manager_utility.cc/.h):**\\n- `cleanInternalHeaders()`: Strips internal-only headers from edge requests and external requests. Removes envoy-prefixed headers (EnvoyDecoratorOperation, EnvoyDownstreamServiceCluster, etc.) that could be injected by untrusted clients.\\n- `sanitizeTEHeader()`: Sanitizes the TE (Transfer-Encoding) header to only allow the 'trailers' value, preventing header injection through this vector.\\n\\n**Connection Header Sanitization (source/common/http/utility.cc):**\\n- `sanitizeConnectionHeader()`: Prevents header injection via the Connection header, which nominates other headers for removal. Enforces a maximum of 10 nominated headers, rejects attempts to nominate pseudo-headers or X-Forwarded-* headers, and validates the TE header size.\\n\\n**Character Set Validation (source/common/http/character_set_validation.h):**\\n- Provides bit-table lookup functions and character set tables (kGenericHeaderNameCharTable, kUriQueryAndFragmentCharTable) compliant with RFC 9110 for efficient header name/value character validation.\\n\\n**Header Validator Extension (source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/):**\\n- Base HeaderValidator class and protocol-specific implementations (http1_header_validator.cc, http2_header_validator.cc) provide extensible header validation.\\n- Validates method, status, path, host, scheme, content-length headers against protocol-specific rules.\\n- `sanitizeHeadersWithUnderscores()`: Handles headers with underscores based on configuration (ALLOW, DROP_HEADER, or REJECT).\\n- Path normalization and percent-encoded sequence checking prevent URL-based injection attacks.\\n\\n**HTTP/1 and HTTP/2 Codec Integration (source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc, http2/codec_impl.cc):**\\n- Both HTTP/1 and HTTP/2 codecs call HeaderUtility::checkValidRequestHeaders() to validate headers at parsing time.\\n- HTTP/1 codec uses Balsa parser (balsa_parser.cc) with validation policies to reject invalid header characters in responses.\\n- HTTP/2 codec integrates nghttp2 header validation to ensure RFC 9113 compliance.\\n\\n**Connection Manager Integration (source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.cc):**\\n- `validateHeaders()`: Calls header_validator_->validateRequestHeaders() to apply header validation rules.\\n- `mutateRequestHeaders()` in ConnectionManagerUtility: Applies all header mutations including sanitization, internal header removal, and port stripping.\\n- Headers are validated on first pass only (is_internally_created check) to prevent bypass for internally-generated requests.\\n\\n**Pseudo-Header Protection:**\\n- Pseudo-headers (HTTP/2 headers starting with ':') are protected from removal and modification through isRemovableHeader() and isModifiableHeader() checks.\\n- These include :authority, :method, :path, :scheme, and :status headers critical to request/response semantics.\\n\\nTogether, these components create defense-in-depth against HTTP header injection by validating character sets, preventing internal header injection, sanitizing dangerous headers, and protecting pseudo-headers from manipulation.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
